***moeten.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:moeten.html>moeten</a> (86)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:moeten.html>moeten</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">muotan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*mōtaną</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">mote</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">may, might</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:moeten.html>moeten</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be necessary, to be required</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">auxiliary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to have to, must
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:moet.html>moet</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:gaan.html>gaan</a>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He <b><a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> to</b> / He <b>must</b> go.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:moest.html>Moest</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nog.html>nog</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:werken.html>werken</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vanavond.html>vanavond</a>?</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><a href = vnd.unilang:did.html>Did</a> you <b>have to</b> work tonight?</span></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verplicht.html>verplicht</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></span></span></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms antonym"><span class="defdate">Antonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoeven.html>hoeven</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">auxiliary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> should, be meant to, be supposed to
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:moet.html>moet</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:hier.html>hier</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gestolen.html>gestolen</a>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">It <b><a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> meant to</b> be here, but it <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stolen.html>stolen</a>. / It <b>should</b> be here, but it <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stolen.html>stolen</a>.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>Dat</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:moet.html>moet</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:echt.html>echt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:doen.html>doen</a>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">You really <b>should</b> not do that.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nieuwe.html>nieuwe</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wet.html>wet</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:moet.html>moet</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> 1 <a href = vnd.unilang:januari.html>januari</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:werking.html>werking</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:treden.html>treden</a>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">The new law <b><a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> supposed to</b> come into force on 1 January.</span></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zou.html>zou</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:moeten.html>moeten</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:horen.html>horen</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to have to go, to need to go, must go
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:moet.html>moet</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:nog.html>nog</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:supermarkt.html>supermarkt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vandaag.html>vandaag</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I still <b>need to go</b> to the supermarket today.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms antonym"><span class="defdate">Antonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoeven.html>hoeven</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to need to go to the <a href = vnd.unilang:toilet.html>toilet</a>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:moet.html>moet</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:heel.html>heel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nodig.html>nodig</a>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I really <b>need to go</b>!</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The past tense <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:moest.html>moest</a></i> can be used in the present. In Dutch, one can ask "<span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:moest.html>Moest</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nog.html>nog</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:werken.html>werken</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vanavond.html>vanavond</a>?</span>" which can mean both "<b><a href = vnd.unilang:did.html>did</a></b> you have to work tonight?" and "<b>do</b> you have to work tonight?". This <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> similar to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gaan.html>gaan</a></i>.</li></ul>

</p>

<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:moet.html>moet</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wc.html>wc</a>.</i> </li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:moetje.html>moetje</a> (5929)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:moetje.html>moetje</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:moetje.html>moetjes</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>a must <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">necessity</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">must</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">especially</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> something that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> necessary but not desired</li>
<li>a shotgun wedding <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">marriage contracted to legitimise a premarital pregnancy</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<p>Shortening of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">moffel</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">moufle</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Latin">Medieval Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">muffula</i>.

***mogen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:mogen.html>mogen</a> (472)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:mogen.html>mogen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">mugan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*maganą</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*magʰ-</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*megʰ-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mogen.html>mogen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be allowed
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hee.html>Hee</a>! <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>Dat</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:mag.html>mag</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><a href = vnd.unilang:hey.html>Hey</a>! <dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toegestaan.html>toegestaan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">auxiliary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> may, can, be allowed to
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:mogen.html>mogen</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:toch.html>toch</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:komen.html>komen</a>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a> <b>can</b> come after all.</span></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kunnen.html>kunnen</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> may go, can go, to be allowed to go
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>Je</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:mag.html>mag</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:buiten.html>buiten</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:veel.html>veel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:koud.html>koud</a>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">You <b>can</b>not <b>go</b> outside, it's far too cold!</span></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kunnen.html>kunnen</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> may have, can have
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:mag.html>Mag</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:twee.html>twee</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:appels.html>appels</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:alstublieft.html>alstublieft</a>?</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>May</b> I <b>have</b> two apples please?</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to like <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">of food or of a person</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">mogentheit</i>. </p>

<p>Related to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">muckezzen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to pout</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">mucken</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to grouse, to grumble</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, ultimately of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Germanic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:West Germanic languages">West Germanic</a></span> onomatopoeic origin.  Probably not related to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">mugio</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">I bellow, <a href = vnd.unilang:moo.html>moo</a>, bray</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***mol.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:mol.html>mol</a> (5820)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_3">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:mol.html>mol</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:mol.html>mol</a></i>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. You can help Wiktionary by elaborating on the origins of this term.</i></span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_8">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mol.html>mol</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mollen.html>mollen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mol.html>molletje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A <span class="Latn" lang="en">mole</span>, any insectivore of the family Talpidae.</li>
<li>A <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/European_mole" class="extiw" title="w:European mole">European mole</a>, <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Talpa_europaea" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Talpa europaea"><i>Talpa europaea</i></a></span>.</li>
<li>A <span class="Latn" lang="en">mole</span>, an <span class="Latn" lang="en">infiltrator</span>, an <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:infiltrant.html>infiltrant</a></span>.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:infiltrant.html>infiltrant</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

***molecuul.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:molecuul.html>molecuul</a> (39197)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">molécule</i>, a modern diminutive of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">moles</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mass</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. First attested in the mid nineteenth century.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:molecuul.html>molecuul</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:moleculen.html>moleculen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:molecuul.html>molecuultje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A molecule, group of atoms <a href = vnd.unilang:held.html>held</a> together by chemical <a href = vnd.unilang:bonds.html>bonds</a>, the smallest natural unit of any given substance</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:moleculair.html>moleculair</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:momo.html>momo</a> (26128)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Standard_Tibetan" class="extiw" title="w:Standard Tibetan">Tibetan</a></span> <i class="Tibt mention" lang="bo">མོག་མོག</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bo-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mog mog</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mandarin_Chinese" class="extiw" title="w:Mandarin Chinese">Mandarin</a></span> <span class="Hani" lang="zh">饃饃</span>／<span class="Hani" lang="zh">馍馍</span> (<i><span class="tr Latn">mómo</span></i>).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:momo.html>momo</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">momos</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A type of Tibetan, Ladakhi and Nepali <a href = vnd.unilang:dumpling.html>dumpling</a> made with a simple flour and water dough.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2007</b> July 1,  “Far East of the <a href = vnd.unilang:u.html>U</a>.N.”, in  <cite>New York Times</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2007/07/01/nyregion/thecity/01rest.html">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Many dishes show a direct influence of China or India; for example, <b>momos</b>, or Tibetan <a href = vnd.unilang:dumplings.html>dumplings</a>, look like Chinese pot-stickers.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
</body>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:monarchie.html>monarchie</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href = vnd.unilang:monarchie.html>monarchie</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">monarchia</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">μοναρχίᾱ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">monarkhíā</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. ***monddood.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:monddood.html>monddood</a> (90557)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mond.html>mond</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dood.html>dood</a></i>, a calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">mundtot</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">silenced</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The term <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> reinterpreted as meaning "dead in the mouth", but it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> originally a legal term meaning “legally incapable”, with the component <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">mund-</i> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh"><a href = vnd.unilang:munt.html>munt</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">protection, guardianship</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*mundō</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:monddood.html>monddood</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">monddoder</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">monddoodst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>silenced, (made) unable to communicate one's thoughts
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>Ze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:monddood.html>monddood</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:gemaakt.html>gemaakt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:anonieme.html>anonieme</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bedreigingen.html>bedreigingen</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">She <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <b>silenced</b> by the anonymous threats.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bijvoeglijk_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:bijvoeglijk.html>Bijvoeglijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:monddood.html>monddood</a></b>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:verhinderen.html>verhinderen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:iemand.html>iemand</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kritiek.html>kritiek</a> of <a href = vnd.unilang:andere.html>andere</a> onwelgevallige <a href = vnd.unilang:informatie.html>informatie</a> bekentmaakt
<dl><dd><ul><li><i> <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:werd.html>werd</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:monddood.html>monddood</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:gemaakt.html>gemaakt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hem.html>hem</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bedreigen.html>bedreigen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gevangenisstraf.html>gevangenisstraf</a>.</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li></ol>

***monding.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:monding.html>monding</a> (51238)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mond.html>mond</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mouth</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ing</i>. Cognate with German Mündung.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:monding.html>monding</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:monding.html>mondingen</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>mouth (of a river or other such current of water)</li></ol>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:riviermond.html>riviermond</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">muide</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***mongool.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:mongool.html>mongool</a> (16223)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mongool.html>Mongool</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">Mongol</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Influenced by <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">mongol</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mongool.html>mongool</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mongolen.html>mongolen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mongooltje.html>mongooltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">vulgar<span class="ib-comma">,</span> offensive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A person with Down's syndrome, a mentally retarded person.
<ul><li><b>1974</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:willem.html>Willem</a> Wilmink, "Frekie".
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:imbeciel.html>imbeciele</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:jongen.html>jongen</a> / <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>Een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:mongool.html>mongool</a></b></i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">He <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> an imbecile boy / A <b>retard</b></span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">vulgar<span class="ib-comma">,</span> offensive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> imbecile, retard</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(demoniem)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:mongool.html>Mongool</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:lid.html>lid</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:etnische.html>etnische</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:groep.html>groep</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:mongolen.html>Mongolen</a>) <a href = vnd.unilang:ontstaan.html>ontstaan</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gebied.html>gebied</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tegenwoordig.html>tegenwoordig</a> Mongolië <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:delen.html>delen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> Rusland <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> China <a href = vnd.unilang:omvat.html>omvat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tweede.html>tweede</a> millennium <a href = vnd.unilang:vanuit.html>vanuit</a> Midden-Azië <a href = vnd.unilang:vele.html>vele</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:rijken.html>rijken</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:veroverde.html>veroverde</a></li>

***mongoose.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:mongoose.html>mongoose</a> (43393)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>1690s. Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Portuguese_language" class="extiw" title="w:Portuguese language">Portuguese</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pt">mangusto</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marathi_language" class="extiw" title="w:Marathi language">Marathi</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="mr">मुंगूस</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="mr-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">muṅgūs</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Marathi_language" class="extiw" title="w:Old Marathi language">Old Marathi</a></span> <i class="Modi mention" lang="omr">𑘦𑘳𑘽𑘐𑘳𑘭</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="omr-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">muṁgusa</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Telugu_language" class="extiw" title="w:Telugu language">Telugu</a></span> <i class="Telu mention" lang="te">ముంగిస</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="te-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">muṅgisa</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Spelling altered by folk-etymological association with <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">goose</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:mongoose.html>mongoose</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">mongooses</b> <i>or</i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">nonstandard</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">mongeese</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Any of several species of generalist predatory Carnivores in the family Herpestidae; the various species range in size from <a href = vnd.unilang:rats.html>rats</a> to large <a href = vnd.unilang:cats.html>cats</a>. The <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Indian_mongoose" class="extiw" title="w:Indian mongoose">Indian <a href = vnd.unilang:mongoose.html>mongoose</a></a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> noted as a predator of venomous <a href = vnd.unilang:snakes.html>snakes</a>, though other <a href = vnd.unilang:mongoose.html>mongoose</a> species have similar habits.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1864</b>,  John Holmes Agnew et <a href = vnd.unilang:al.html>al</a>.,  <cite>The Eclectic Magazine: Foreign Literature</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=42itff9BcjoCamp;pg=PA334">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">After the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:mongoose.html>mongoose</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> satisfied its appetite, <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> proceeded to examine with a pocket lens the wounds he <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> received from the <a href = vnd.unilang:cobra.html>cobra</a>; and on cleansing one of these <a href = vnd.unilang:places.html>places</a>, the lens disclosed <i>the broken fang of the <a href = vnd.unilang:cobra.html>cobra</a> deeply imbedded in the head of the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:mongoose.html>mongoose</a></b>...</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a> have <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:mongoose.html>mongoose</a></b> confined ever since (now four days' time), and it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> as healthy and lively as ever.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1924</b>,  Rudyard Kipling,  <cite>The <a href = vnd.unilang:jungle.html>Jungle</a> Book:Rikki-Tikki-Tavi</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">He <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:mongoose.html>mongoose</a></b>, rather like a little cat in his fur and his tail, but quite like a weasel in his head and his habits.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>Any species of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Malagasy_mongoose" class="extiw" title="w:Malagasy mongoose">Malagasy mongooses</a>; only distantly related to the Herpestidae, these are members of the family Eupleridae; they resemble mongooses in appearance and habits, but have larger ears and ringed <a href = vnd.unilang:tails.html>tails</a>.</li></ol>
</body>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:monnik.html>monnik</a> (6981)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">monic</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*monik</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vulgar_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Vulgar Latin">Vulgar Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">monicus</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Latin">Medieval Latin</a></span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">monachus</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">μοναχός</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">monakhós</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">single, solitary</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">μόνος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mónos</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">alone</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Mönch</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">monk</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>monk</li></ol>

***monnikskap.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:monnikskap.html>monnikskap</a> (40487)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:monnik.html>monnik</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">monk</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-s-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kap.html>kap</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cap, hood</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:monnikskap.html>monnikskap</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:monnikskap.html>monnikskappen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:monnikskap.html>monnikskapje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literally</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A monk's hood, notably part of his habit</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">botany</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The herbs known as monkshood, of genus <i>Aconitum</i>; notably the very toxic species <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Aconitum_napellus" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Aconitum napellus"><i>Aconitum napellus</i></a></span> and its ornamental cultivars</li></ol>

<ul><li>(botany) <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:akoniet.html>akoniet</a></span></li></ul>

<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">monnikspij</span></li>

***monster.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:monster.html>monster</a> (1365)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">monstrum</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:monster.html>monster</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:monster.html>monster</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:monsters.html>monsters</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:monstertje.html>monstertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A <a href="English"><a href = vnd.unilang:monster.html>monster</a></a>, terrifying and dangerous creature.</li>
<li>An extremely antisocial person, especially a criminal.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">muster</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:monster.html>monster</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:monsters.html>monsters</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:monstertje.html>monstertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">sample</span>; small, representative quantity of a substance or material, as used for analysis or selection.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:inspectie.html>inspectie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nam.html>nam</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:monster.html>monster</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> water.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The inspection <a href = vnd.unilang:took.html>took</a> a <b>sample</b> of the water.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hebben.html>hebben</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:monsters.html>monsters</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:alle.html>alle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:soorten.html>soorten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:behang.html>behang</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a> have <b><a href = vnd.unilang:samples.html>samples</a></b> of all <a href = vnd.unilang:types.html>types</a> of wallpaper.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
